# LINE emoji

**Source:** https://developers.line.biz/en/docs/messaging-api/emoji-list/
**Section:** Messaging API

**Description:** A searchable list of LINE emoji IDs and code points for use in the Messaging API.

class="sidebar-group mb-3 pb-3 transition border-b border-ldsgray-300 dark:border-ldsgray-700 border-b-0" data-v-6bc7ccd9 data-v-e2dd214b><a href="#" class="text-black dark:text-white hover:opacity-60 custom sidebar-heading flex justify-between py-2 transition text-caption-docs-side-title" data-v-e2dd214b><span data-v-e2dd214b>Case studies</span><span class="block h-5 w-5 flex-shrink-0 flex justify-center items-center" data-v-e2dd214b><span class="la-rotate-270 las la-chevron-left text-xs transition-transform" data-v-e2dd214b></span></span></a><!----></section></li><!--]--></ul></div><div class="content-container 2xl:mt-0 mt-[80px] lg:grid lg:gap-[60px]" style="grid-template-columns:1fr 180px;" data-v-4dba8b53><div class="content-with-sidebars" data-v-4dba8b53><!--[--><!--[--><main class="markdown-content"><div><h1 id class="text-4xl text-highlighted font-bold mb-8 scroll-mt-[calc(45px+var(--ui-header-height))] lg:scroll-mt-(--ui-header-height)"><!--[-->LINE emoji<!--]--></h1><p><!--[-->Using the Messaging API, you can use LINE emoji in text messages. For instructions to send text messages, see <a href="/en/docs/messaging-api/sending-messages/" class=""><!--[--><!--[-->Send messages<!--]--><!--]--></a>.<!--]--></p><div class="danger custom-block"><div class="custom-block-title"><i class="las la-exclamation-triangle mr-2"></i><span>&quot;LINE original unicode emojis&quot; is discontinued as of March 31, 2022</span></div><div><!--[--><p><!--[-->Instead of &quot;LINE original unicode emojis&quot;, use LINE emoji with the <code><!--[-->emojis<!--]--></code> property. For more information, see the news from April 1, 2022, <a href="/en/news/2022/04/01/line-original-unicode-emojis-has-been-discontinued/" class=""><!--[--><!--[-->&quot;LINE original unicode emojis&quot; of the Messaging API has been discontinued as of March 31, 2022<!--]--><!--]--></a>.<!--]--></p><!--]--></div></div><div class="warning custom-block"><div class="custom-block-title"><i class="las la-exclamation-circle mr-2"></i><span>Supported emoji types in text messages</span></div><div><!--[--><p><!--[-->In <a href="/en/reference/messaging-api/#text-message" class=""><!--[--><!--[-->text messages<!--]--><!--]--></a> and <a href="/en/reference/messaging-api/#text-message-v2" class=""><!--[--><!--[-->text messages (v2)<!--]--><!--]--></a>, you can use Unicode emoji in addition to LINE emoji.<!--]--></p><table><!--[--><thead><!--[--><tr><!--[--><th><!--[-->Emoji type<!--]--></th><th><!--[-->Object type<!--]--></th><th><!--[-->How to use<!--]--></th><!--]--></tr><!--]--></thead><tbody><!--[--><tr><!--[--><td><!--[-->LINE emoji<!--]--></td><td><!--[-->Text message<!--]--></td><td><!--[-->Specify the emoji&#39;s product ID and emoji ID in the <code><!--[-->emojis<!--]--></code> property.<!--]--></td><!--]--></tr><tr><!--[--><td><!--[-->LINE emoji<!--]--></td><td><!--[-->Text message (v2)<!--]--></td><td><!--[-->Specify the emoji&#39;s product ID and emoji ID in the <a href="/en/reference/messaging-api/#text-message-v2-emoji-object" class=""><!--[--><!--[-->emoji object<!--]--><!--]--></a>.<!--]--></td><!--]--></tr><tr><!--[--><td><!--[-->Unicode emoji<!--]--></td><td><!--[--><ul><!--[--><li><!--[-->Text message<!--]--></li><li><!--[-->Text message (v2)<!--]--></li><!--]--></ul><!--]--></td><td><!--[-->Enter emoji as they are or enter Unicode code points in the <code><!--[-->text<!--]--></code> property.<!--]--></td><!--]--></tr><!--]--></tbody><!--]--></table><!--]--></div></div><h2 class="relative"><div id="specify-emojis-in-message-object" class="w-px h-px absolute -top-40 -left-1"></div><a href="#specify-emojis-in-message-object" class="text-inherit custom markdown-header-anchor hover:no-underline" data-v-16f80a9e><!--[--><!--[-->Specify LINE emojis in message objects<!--]--><!--]--></a></h2><p><!--[-->To send an emoji, specify the product ID and emoji ID of the emoji in a <a href="/en/reference/messaging-api/#text-message" class=""><!--[--><!--[-->text message<!--]--><!--]--></a> object or <a href="/en/reference/messaging-api/#text-message-v2" class=""><!--[--><!--[-->text message (v2)<!--]--><!--]--></a> object. For example, when using a text message, specify the <code><!--[-->emojis.productId<!--]--></code> and <code><!--[-->emojis.emojiId<!--]--></code> properties as shown in the figure below:<!--]--></p><p><!--[--><!--[--><!----><!----><!--[--><img src="/media/messaging-api/emojis-object/emojis-object-en.png" alt class="w-auto will-change-transform cursor-zoom-in w-fix-960 border rounded-sm p-2" type="button" aria-haspopup="dialog" aria-expanded="false" data-state="closed"><!--v-if--><!--]--><!--]--><!--]--></p><h2 class="relative"><div id="line-emoji-definitions" class="w-px h-px absolute -top-40 -left-1"></div><a href="#line-emoji-definitions" class="text-inherit custom markdown-header-anchor hover:no-underline" data-v-16f80a9e><!--[--><!--[-->LINE emoji definitions<!--]--><!--]--></a></h2><p><!--[-->The number attached to each LINE emoji is the emoji&#39;s emoji ID.<!--]--></p><div data-v-537568e6><!--[--><div class="sm:p-3 py-10 my-4 border-t
